This means you’ll have great shopping and nightlife options right at your doorstep, in addition to being able to get to your campus quickly. Especially the Liverpool John Moores University city campus is really close by, just a 5-minute walk away. Each of the housing types offers diverse level of privacy, facility, cost, and living experience, and you can choose one of them according to your own preferences and requirements. For you convenience, we list the key features of the main popular types of Liverpool student housing as below:\n\n...\n\n#### Purpose-Built Student Accommodations (PBSAs)\n* **Features:** PBSAs are the modern apartments specially designed for students, typically located within walking or short bus ride to the campus or in the City Centre and student-friendly areas. Moreover, there are ample upscale communal amenities and social spaces, such as on-site, gym, laundry facilities, study rooms, rooftop terrace, and lounges. Renting Shared Private Houses (HMOs) or Private Apartments means you will have a private bedroom with shared kitchen, bathroom, and living room. Utility bills are not included in the rent, but you can share the rent with other roommate to save money on housing rentals. Lease term is also flexible and can be negotiated.\n* **Average Rent: £90 - £150 per week.**\n* **Examples:** 65 Hall Lane, and Pall Mall Press Liverpool.\n\n#### Studio Apartments\n* **Features:** A studio is a self-contained open-area apartment with bedroom area, kitchenette and separate bathroom. Studio offers you the complete privacy and independence, and the rent of some studio choices is cheaper than one-bedroom apartment. Studio Apartments also welcome couples to live in.\n* **Average Rent: £150 - £250 per week.**\n* **Examples: Maple House** , and Lennon Studios.\n\n#### Homestays/Resident Landlord\n* **Features:** Choosing Homestays/Resident Landlord means you are going to live with a host family, which is a great choice for international students to improve foreign language and immerse yourselves in the local culture. Property details

## Grand Central is in a great city-centre location, right next to Liverpool Lime Street rail station. It’s just eight minutes’ walk to LJMU and only 10 minutes to the University of Liverpool.

Read More

-   Address:
    
    Skelhorne Street, Liverpool, L3 5GA
    
    View map
-   Distance to Liverpool John Moores University:
    
    -   7mins
    -   4mins
    
-   Distance to Liverpool John Moores University(City Campus):
    
    -   12mins
    -   13mins
    -   8mins
    
-   Free cancellation period:
    
    Within 7 calendar days
    
-   Facilities: Furnished, Laundry+8
    
-   Bills included: WiFi, Water, Electricity, Heating, Gas+1
    

We’ve got a wide range of rooms available here. We’ve got rooms in shared flats with shared bathrooms and kitchens, en-suite rooms with a private bathroom, and self-contained studios where you get your own bathroom and kitchen. The choice is yours.

With over 1,200 neighbours, you’ll never be short of company. The common room at Grand Central contains a sofa and TV area (complete with PS4), table football, ping pong, pool table, and free tea and coffee.

At Grand Central, you’re not just minutes away from your university. You’re also right beside Liverpool’s world-class museums, galleries, theatres, and shopping districts.

### **\*1st-year students at Liverpool John Moore University will need to apply through the University for this property.**

## Booking process

Submit an application

Speak with your consultant

Booking confirmation

**Submit an application:** Let us know your request needs and contact information. Don't worry if you're unsure of your dates/school yet, just let us know

**Speak with your consultant:** You'll be paired with a specialized booking consultant, ask away! Let him/her know more about what you're looking for

**Booking confirmation:** Complete the booking application form and other property-specific documents, and then we'll help you confirm your booking

## Booking Terms

Book With Confidence

No Visa No Pay:Your booking can be cancelled for free if the Visa application has been deniedNo Place No Pay:A booking can be cancelled for free if you have failed to obtain the required qualifications to get into your university of choice

If you need to cancel your reservation, please apply within 7 days after the deposit is paid, otherwise the deposit cannot be refunded.

Cancellation Policy

**The booking**

Once a booking is processed, the student has 3 days to accept the offer. It means for the student and the guarantor to accept the contract and pay the £250 advance rent payment. (For bookings in England only. No Advance Rent Payment is required for bookings in Scotland).

Once these steps are done, the booking is completed.

If one of the step is not completed within these 3 days, the offer will expire.

If the student still wants a room, we can re-process a booking, but we cannot guarantee that the same room or the same price will be available.

Once the booking is completed, the student has another 7 days to change their mind and cancel their booking without any reasons. This is called the cooling-off period.

**Conditions for cancellation**

Past these 7 days, the student remains liable for the rent for the whole length of the tenancy unless they want to cancel with one of these 3 conditions:

·       **No Place No Pay:** if the student fails their exams or is rejected by the UK University, the student needs to send us the university rejection letter, or proof that the exam results don’t meet the requirements of the university, and we will cancel the booking and refund the money to the student. The student must send us the proof documents within 7 days of receiving them. This policy is valid until the **15th September.**

·       **No Visa No Pay:** if the student doesn’t get their visa to come and study in the UK, the student must send us the visa application rejection letter within 7 days of receiving it and we will cancel the booking and refund the money to the student. This policy is valid until the 15th September.

·       **No ATAS certificate, No Pay:** Some international students coming to the UK to study in very specific fields need to apply for an ATAS certificate. (Academic Technology Approval Scheme). If a student’s ATAS certificate application is rejected we will cancel the booking and refund the money to the student. The student must send us the ATAS certificate application rejection letter within 7 days of receiving it and we will cancel the booking and refund the money to the student. This policy is valid until the 15th September.

The cancellation requests along with the proof documents must be sent by the student, from the email address they have registered their account with Unite Students.

The email must be sent either from the student to the agent, and then the agent contacts our teams.

**Replacement tenant found:** if the student finds a replacement tenant to take over his room with the same tenancy length and same weekly rate, we can process the booking for the new student, and once the offer has been accepted by the new student and his guarantor, and that they have paid the £250 (if applicable), we will release the original student from their contract.

Passed the 15th September, the No Place No Pay and No Visa No Pay do not apply.

The student remains liable for the rent unless they find a replacement.

For more information, please refer to the property's terms & conditions. The property reserves the right to interpret and modify the terms with sole discretion.

Liverpool Student Housing

# Find student housing in Liverpool

At Student.com you can find and compare student accommodation in Liverpool. Whether you’re looking for a shared or a private room or a fully self-contained studio, you can find your ideal student home here. Talk to one of our booking consultants if you want to find out more.

Sort by: Recommended

Sort by: Recommended

AboutUniversities

Explore Liverpool

About

## Student accommodation in Liverpool

With a large student population and a cultural scene that delivers in spades, Liverpool is one of the most loved student cities in the UK. The city is considered one of the most affordable in the region and Student.com can help you easily find the right student housing for your budget.

  

You can use our search filters to narrow down the options and find your perfect student home. Whether you want to live in the city centre or right next to your university, our range of student accommodation in Liverpool caters to everyone.

  

**Start browsing at the top of the page – or continue reading to learn more about student life on Merseyside! If you need any more information, you can always give us a call or talk to us via the live chat function.**

## Universities in Liverpool

Liverpool is home to two world-class universities in the University of Liverpool and Liverpool John Moores University, while it also has a host of other institutions offering specialised courses.

### University of Liverpool

Liverpool’s biggest university by enrolment, the University of Liverpool has almost 30,000 students – of whom roughly 10,000 are from abroad. It's a member of the prestigious Russell Group and regularly ranks among the top 150 universities in the world.

  

The main campus is based just a short walk from the city centre – ideal for exploring Liverpool. The university boasts strong subject rankings across the board, but is especially well known for business, engineering and life sciences.

  

**Joining the ranks of Liverpool’s biggest university? Get browsing our amazing** [**University of Liverpool accommodation**](https://web.archive.org/web/20251104075917/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/university-of-liverpool)**!** 

### Liverpool John Moores University

Liverpool John Moores University (LJMU) has about 25,000 students, over 3,000 of whom are from outside the UK. So, if you’re looking for an international atmosphere while studying, you’ll be sure to find it here.

  

LJMU places strong emphasis on career skills, with lots of courses involving work placements. It has an amazing reputation for sports science and exercise, while it’s also a great option for engineering.

  

**Heading to Liverpool’s other major university? We have an excellent selection of** [**LJMU accommodation**](https://web.archive.org/web/20251104075917/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/liverpool-john-moores-university) **available!** 

### Liverpool Hope University

Home to around 5,000 students, Liverpool Hope University is a smaller institution with a rich history dating back to 1844. It’s based on the eastern fringes of the city, offering a more relaxed feel than the other two universities.

  

The university boasts strong student satisfaction rates and offers a wide range of programmes, with key strengths in arts, humanities and education.

  

**Like the sound of this university? Check out our** [**accommodation for Liverpool Hope University**](https://web.archive.org/web/20251104075917/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/liverpool-hope-university)**!** 

## Things for students to do in Liverpool

There are several things that make Liverpool a great city to study in. It’s laid-back, fun and affordable, and if you want to have a great party after a long week of studying, Liverpool is definitely the place for you. 

### Arts & culture

Liverpool is a cultural hotspot. Outside of [London](https://web.archive.org/web/20251104075917/https://www.student.com/uk/london), it has more museums and art galleries than any city in the UK. From Tate Liverpool and its world-famous collection of modern art to the live music and performances of East Village’s Arts Club and RIBA award-winning theatre the Everyman – just to name a few – it has cultural interests to meet all needs.

  

The city also has the oldest Chinese community in Europe. The cultural vibrancy of Liverpool really adds to the student experience, allowing newcomers to easily connect and interact with the city and its inhabitants.

### History

With a grand backdrop of Victorian and Georgian buildings, Liverpool is a vibrant city that celebrates its glorious past. And it’s always looking to innovate, too – take the famous ‘Bombed Out Church’ which has been transformed into a concert venue as an example.

The city is home to many famous landmarks such as the homes of The Beatles members, the Liver Buildings, and the historic docks – all of which will become familiar sights if you choose to study in the city.

### Sport

A huge part of Liverpool’s worldwide fame is thanks to its football. It’s home to one of the sport's most famous rivalries, the Merseyside Derby between Liverpool and Everton, two storied clubs in the English Premier League. Liverpool FC is one of the most successful teams in England and Europe.

  

Even if you’re not a hardcore football fan, don’t miss out on the chance to see a Premier League game at one of the city’s famous stadiums – you can be sure the atmosphere will be great.

### Nightlife

Liverpool is known for its laid-back way of life – but it comes alive at night. There are bars galore from Concert Square all the way to the Cavern Quarter. If you're looking for a good student night out, there’s somewhere to go each day of the week.

  

The warehouse scene in the Baltic Triangle provides several options, while Secret bars like Berry and Rye and Ex-Directory provide less-than-typical experiences.

  

Smithdown Road is home to a large percentage of Liverpool's 60,000-plus student population and is always brimming with energy. Here you can have fun with fellow students and enjoy cheap pints at the city’s long-established student quarter. 

## Best student areas in Liverpool

When it comes to student housing in Liverpool, there are a handful of [key areas that most students look to target](https://web.archive.org/web/20251104075917/https://www.student.com/articles/best-student-areas-liverpool). 

### Smithdown Road

Stretching from Edge Hill just east of the city centre through Wavertree and Picton, Smithdown Road serves as Liverpool’s main student hub.

  

Here you’ll find lots of students from the University of Liverpool and LJMU. There’s plenty of affordable accommodation available in the form of converted student flats. 

### City centre

The city centre is another popular choice for students as it puts you right on the doorstep of Liverpool’s top attractions while still being close to the two main universities.

  

Modern, purpose-built student complexes are common, which often come with flashy amenities like on-site gyms, but generally command a higher price. 

### Kensington

Kensington is just a short walk east of the city centre and another contender for student living. Again, it’s convenient for both University of Liverpool and LJMU students.

  

Like Smithdown Road, it’s mostly made up of terraced housing, offering great value and that classic UK student experience. 

## Student cost of living in Liverpool

One of the most important aspects of choosing a city for university is its affordability, and Liverpool is one of the most affordable cities in the UK.

  

Student discounts are offered in most bars and clubs, and if you happen to take a cab or bus to get there, it won’t cost you as much as transport is very affordable. 

### Free things to do in Liverpool

Many of Liverpool’s museums and art galleries offer free admission, including Tate Liverpool, Walker Art Gallery, Merseyside Maritime Museum, World Museum and the Museum of Liverpool.

  

The Albert Docks, home to award-winning attractions like the Beatles Story and the International Slavery Museum, often has free events. 

### Student discounts in Liverpool

Many of the big-name shops in Liverpool’s compact central shopping district provide student discounts ranging from 10% to 20%.

  

You can also sign up to discount platforms like UNiDAYS and Student Beans using your student ID to unlock additional discounts throughout the city. 

## Public transport in Liverpool

Getting around Liverpool is easy thanks to the city’s comprehensive public transport system, which includes buses, trams and even ferries! 

### Rail

The local Merseyrail system encompasses a mix of underground and overground stations for navigating the city centre and surrounding areas. You can also easily reach other major UK cities like Manchester and London via the national rail system. 

### Bus

The bus is the affordable way to get around town and covers areas not directly served by the rail system, with stops conveniently placed near all three of the city’s universities. 

### Ferry

For a more scenic way to travel, Mersey Ferries runs regular services across the river between Liverpool and Wirral. These are great for sightseeing along the waterfront. 

## Frequently asked questions

### Is Liverpool a safe place for students to live?

Liverpool is indeed a safe city for students. It’s well-lit and well-known for its friendly atmosphere, while it also has various safety initiatives in place. Popular student areas like Smithdown Road and Kensington are especially safe, but, as in any major city, you should still exercise basic precautions. 

### Is there a high demand for student housing in Liverpool?

Liverpool’s large student population means the demand for accommodation is consistently high – particularly in key student hubs like Smithdown Road and Kensington. The most desirable properties are usually booked by early spring, so it’s best to start your search early in the new year to avoid disappointment. 

### How much does student housing in Liverpool cost?

Student accommodation in Liverpool is generally a lot cheaper than in other major UK cities. At the lower end of the scale, a room in a shared student house in an area like Smithdown Road may cost as little as £80 per week, while a private apartment in the city centre will generally be around £150 per week. 

### Where are the best areas for students in Liverpool?

Smithdown Road has long served as Liverpool’s main student area, with nearby Kensington also popular and offering a similar vibe. The city centre is also popular and has a host of modern student residences, though these tend to be considerably more expensive than flats in the city’s outlying neighbourhoods. 

### Do I need a visa to study abroad in Liverpool?

Yes, if you’re planning on studying at a university in Liverpool as a non-UK or Irish citizen, you’ll need to apply for a student visa before you start your course. You can learn more about the requirements and application process [here](https://web.archive.org/web/20251104075917/https://www.gov.uk/student-visa). 

### What if I didn’t get an answer to my question here?

For information on how the booking process works, click [here](https://web.archive.org/web/20251104075917/https://www.student.com/how-it-works). We also have answers to a range of other questions on our [FAQ page](https://web.archive.org/web/20251104075917/https://www.student.com/help). If you still haven’t found what you’re looking for, don’t hesitate to contact us!

From Tate Liverpool and its world-famous collection of modern art to the live music and performances of East Village’s Arts Club and RIBA award-winning theatre the Everyman – just to name a few – it has cultural interests to meet all needs.

  

The city also has the oldest Chinese community in Europe. The cultural vibrancy of Liverpool really adds to the student experience, allowing newcomers to easily connect and interact with the city and its inhabitants.

### History

With a grand backdrop of Victorian and Georgian buildings, Liverpool is a vibrant city that celebrates its glorious past. And it’s always looking to innovate, too – take the famous ‘Bombed Out Church’ which has been transformed into a concert venue as an example.

The city is home to many famous landmarks such as the homes of The Beatles members, the Liver Buildings, and the historic docks – all of which will become familiar sights if you choose to study in the city.

### Sport

A huge part of Liverpool’s worldwide fame is thanks to its football. It’s home to one of the sport's most famous rivalries, the Merseyside Derby between Liverpool and Everton, two storied clubs in the English Premier League. Liverpool FC is one of the most successful teams in England and Europe.

  

Even if you’re not a hardcore football fan, don’t miss out on the chance to see a Premier League game at one of the city’s famous stadiums – you can be sure the atmosphere will be great.

### Nightlife

Liverpool is known for its laid-back way of life – but it comes alive at night. There are bars galore from Concert Square all the way to the Cavern Quarter. If you're looking for a good student night out, there’s somewhere to go each day of the week.

  

The warehouse scene in the Baltic Triangle provides several options, while Secret bars like Berry and Rye and Ex-Directory provide less-than-typical experiences.

  

Smithdown Road is home to a large percentage of Liverpool's 60,000-plus student population and is always brimming with energy. Here you can have fun with fellow students and enjoy cheap pints at the city’s long-established student quarter. 

## Best student areas in Liverpool

When it comes to student housing in Liverpool, there are a handful of [key areas that most students look to target](https://web.archive.org/web/20251104075917/https://www.student.com/articles/best-student-areas-liverpool). 

### Smithdown Road

Stretching from Edge Hill just east of the city centre through Wavertree and Picton, Smithdown Road serves as Liverpool’s main student hub.

  

Here you’ll find lots of students from the University of Liverpool and LJMU. There’s plenty of affordable accommodation available in the form of converted student flats. 

### City centre

The city centre is another popular choice for students as it puts you right on the doorstep of Liverpool’s top attractions while still being close to the two main universities.

  

Modern, purpose-built student complexes are common, which often come with flashy amenities like on-site gyms, but generally command a higher price. 

### Kensington

Kensington is just a short walk east of the city centre and another contender for student living. Again, it’s convenient for both University of Liverpool and LJMU students.

  

Like Smithdown Road, it’s mostly made up of terraced housing, offering great value and that classic UK student experience. 

## Student cost of living in Liverpool

One of the most important aspects of choosing a city for university is its affordability, and Liverpool is one of the most affordable cities in the UK.

  

Student discounts are offered in most bars and clubs, and if you happen to take a cab or bus to get there, it won’t cost you as much as transport is very affordable. 

### Free things to do in Liverpool

Many of Liverpool’s museums and art galleries offer free admission, including Tate Liverpool, Walker Art Gallery, Merseyside Maritime Museum, World Museum and the Museum of Liverpool.

  

The Albert Docks, home to award-winning attractions like the Beatles Story and the International Slavery Museum, often has free events. 

### Student discounts in Liverpool

Many of the big-name shops in Liverpool’s compact central shopping district provide student discounts ranging from 10% to 20%.

  

You can also sign up to discount platforms like UNiDAYS and Student Beans using your student ID to unlock additional discounts throughout the city. 

## Public transport in Liverpool

Getting around Liverpool is easy thanks to the city’s comprehensive public transport system, which includes buses, trams and even ferries! 

### Rail

The local Merseyrail system encompasses a mix of underground and overground stations for navigating the city centre and surrounding areas. You can also easily reach other major UK cities like Manchester and London via the national rail system. 

### Bus

The bus is the affordable way to get around town and covers areas not directly served by the rail system, with stops conveniently placed near all three of the city’s universities. 

### Ferry

For a more scenic way to travel, Mersey Ferries runs regular services across the river between Liverpool and Wirral. These are great for sightseeing along the waterfront. 

## Frequently asked questions

### Is Liverpool a safe place for students to live?

Liverpool is indeed a safe city for students. It’s well-lit and well-known for its friendly atmosphere, while it also has various safety initiatives in place. Popular student areas like Smithdown Road and Kensington are especially safe, but, as in any major city, you should still exercise basic precautions. 

### Is there a high demand for student housing in Liverpool?

Liverpool’s large student population means the demand for accommodation is consistently high – particularly in key student hubs like Smithdown Road and Kensington. The most desirable properties are usually booked by early spring, so it’s best to start your search early in the new year to avoid disappointment. 

### How much does student housing in Liverpool cost?

Student accommodation in Liverpool is generally a lot cheaper than in other major UK cities. At the lower end of the scale, a room in a shared student house in an area like Smithdown Road may cost as little as £80 per week, while a private apartment in the city centre will generally be around £150 per week. 

### Where are the best areas for students in Liverpool?

Smithdown Road has long served as Liverpool’s main student area, with nearby Kensington also popular and offering a similar vibe. The city centre is also popular and has a host of modern student residences, though these tend to be considerably more expensive than flats in the city’s outlying neighbourhoods. 

### Do I need a visa to study abroad in Liverpool?

Yes, if you’re planning on studying at a university in Liverpool as a non-UK or Irish citizen, you’ll need to apply for a student visa before you start your course. You can learn more about the requirements and application process [here](https://web.archive.org/web/20251104075917/https://www.gov.uk/student-visa). 

### What if I didn’t get an answer to my question here?

For information on how the booking process works, click [here](https://web.archive.org/web/20251104075917/https://www.student.com/how-it-works). We also have answers to a range of other questions on our [FAQ page](https://web.archive.org/web/20251104075917/https://www.student.com/help). If you still haven’t found what you’re looking for, don’t hesitate to contact us!

## Liverpool International College

## Student accommodation in Liverpool

With a large student population and culture and nightlife scenes that deliver attractive options in spades, Liverpool is one of the most loved student cities in the UK. The city is considered one of the most affordable in the region and Student.com can help you easily find the right student accommodation for your budget.

You can utilise our search filters to find your favourite from more than 50 different student accommodation options in Liverpool. You can also use our mapping tool to find apartments in the area of the city you like, whether you want to live in the city centre or right next to your university.

If you need any more information, you can always give us a call or talk to us via the live chat function. Our booking consultants are always happy to help you and answer any questions you may have.

## Liverpool at a glance

Liverpool, hometown of the legendary Beatles, is a city and metropolitan borough in Merseyside, England. In addition to one of the most influential bands of all time, this iconic city has a lot of other things to offer as well.

With a grand backdrop of Victorian and Georgian buildings, it’s an intimate and vibrant city that celebrates its glorious past. It’s home to many famous landmarks such as the homes of The Beatles members, The Liver Buildings, and the historic docks – all of which will become familiar sights if you choose to study in the city.

The city also values friendship. Liverpool is one of the friendliest cities in the UK and the third best to visit worldwide according to the Rough Guides guidebooks. Whether the local people are helping you find your way around the city, or just having a chat, the Scousers, as they’re affectionately called, will make your time in the city a memorable one.

### Football in Liverpool

A huge part of Liverpool’s worldwide fame is thanks to its football. Liverpool is proud of its undying love for the sport. It’s home to one of football's most famous rivalries, the Merseyside Derby between Liverpool and Everton, two storied clubs in the English Premier League. Liverpool FC is one of the most successful teams in England and Europe.

Even if you’re not a hardcore football fan, don’t miss out on the chance to see a Premier League game at one of the city’s famous stadiums, Liverpool FC’s Anfield or Everton’s Goodison Park. You can be sure that the atmosphere will be great.

### A city of culture

Liverpool is a cultural hotspot. Outside of London, it has more museums and art galleries than any city in the UK. From the Tate Modern and its world-famous collection of modern art to the live music and performances of The East Village Arts Club and the RIBA award-winning theatre The Everyman, just to name a few, it has cultural interests to meet all needs.

Liverpool wears its culture proudly. This a city that turned it’s bombed-out church into a concert venue, and has a night specifically dedicated to wandering around and looking at various light installations throughout the city.

The city also has the oldest Chinese community in Europe. The cultural vibrancy of Liverpool augments its environment, allowing new students to easily connect and interact with the city.

## Student life in Liverpool

There are several things that make Liverpool a great city to study in. It’s laid-back, fun and affordable, and if you want to have a great party after a long week of studying, Liverpool is definitely the place for you.

### Liverpool is an affordable city

One of the most important aspects of choosing a city to study in is its affordability. Liverpool is one of the most affordable cities in the UK. There are student discounts offered in most bars and clubs and if you happen to have to take a cab or bus to get there it won’t cost you much as taxis and buses are very affordable. Buses also run frequently so you won’t be stuck waiting for ages.

### Free museums and student discounts

Many of Liverpool’s museums and art galleries can be entered for free by students including Tate Liverpool, Walker Art Gallery, Merseyside Maritime Museum, World Museum and the Museum of Liverpool. The Albert Docks, home to award-winning attractions like The Beatles Story and The International Slavery Museum, always has free events.

Many of the big-name shops in Liverpool’s compact central shopping district provide student discounts ranging from 10% to 20%.

### Great nightlife

Liverpool is known for its laid-back way of life but it comes alive at night. Its vibrant nightlife offers many choices for all tastes. There are bars galore from Concert Square all the way to the Cavern Quarter. If you're looking for a good student night out there’s somewhere to go for each day of the week.

There are many music venues where you can listen to some live music ranging from the most in-demand musicians to up-and-coming artists. If you prefer a less-than-typical night out experience, the warehouse scene in the Baltic Triangle provides several options. Alma de Cuba, a bar in a former church, as well as the multitude of secret bars like Berry and Rye and Ex-Directory also provide less-than-typical experiences.

A large part of Liverpool’s nightlife is centred around three main areas - the centre of town, Lark Lane and the Baltic Triangle, where you’ll find some of the best cocktails, live music, and general revelry.

However, Smithdown Road, whose junction with Penny Lane is the subject of the Beatles song "Penny Lane," is home to a large percentage of Liverpool's 60,000-plus university student population and is always brimming with energy. Here you can have fun with fellow students as well as some delightful local Scousers at the Evil Eye Burrito Shack and cheap pints at Brookhouse on Thursdays at the long-established student quarter.

Overall, Liverpool’s nightlife is student-friendly. Venues are easy to get to as the majority of the student bars are within walking distance of each other.

## Universities in Liverpool

Liverpool is home to two world-class universities, with both the University of Liverpool and Liverpool John Moores University featured in the QS World University Rankings.

The University of Liverpool has almost 30,000 students, of whom almost 10,000 are from abroad. It was ranked as the 190th best university in the world in the 2023 QS World University Rankings.

Liverpool John Moores University has about 25,000 students, over 3,000 of whom are from outside the UK. So, if you’re looking for an international atmosphere while studying, you’ll be sure to find it here. John Moores was also ranked as one of the 1,000 best universities in the world by QS in their 2023 rankings.

In addition to these two, there are also numerous colleges and the famous Liverpool Institute for Performing Arts. Some of the most famous institutions of higher learning in Liverpool include:

-   [University of Liverpool](https://web.archive.org/web/20240806193152/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/university-of-liverpool)
-   [Liverpool John Moores University](https://web.archive.org/web/20240806193152/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/liverpool-john-moores-university-main-campus)
-   [Liverpool Hope University](https://web.archive.org/web/20240806193152/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/liverpool-hope-university)
-   [Liverpool Institute for Performing Arts](https://web.archive.org/web/20240806193152/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/liverpool-institute-for-performing-arts)
-   [Liverpool International College](https://web.archive.org/web/20240806193152/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/liverpool-international-college)

## Frequently asked questions about student housing in Liverpool

### How do I apply for student accommodation on Student.com?

Booking a student residence in Liverpool is free and easy on Student.com. After you’ve found your ideal uni accommodation in Liverpool, click ‘View rooms’ to go to the property page. There you’ll need to choose your preferred room type and click ‘Enquire’ or ‘Book Now.’

One of our booking consultants will then contact you to take you through the next steps and answer any questions you may have.

### What are the different room types you offer?

We currently offer two different types of rooms that you can choose from in Liverpool.

In a Private Room, you’ll get your own private bedroom and, in some properties, a private bathroom as well. However, in some properties, the bathroom is shared. Additional facilities like the kitchen will be shared.

Booking the Entire Place will give you a fully self-contained studio property with your own bedroom, bathroom and usually a small kitchenette for cooking meals. No need to share with anyone, so this option is perfect if you love your own space!

### Can I live together with a friend?

Yes. Tell your booking consultant that you’d like to live with a friend, and we can arrange this. Make sure your friend does the same when making their booking as well.

### Can I see the property before I move in?

Many of the properties we list have a great range of photos, videos and even virtual tours that will give you a great idea of what your new home will look like. So, even if you can’t make it to a viewing before moving in, you don’t have to worry, as you’ll be able to get a good idea of what your new home will look like.

If you’ll be in Liverpool before your move-in date and would prefer to see the place for yourself though, this can be arranged as well. Just get in touch with us and our booking consultants will set up a viewing for you.

### How do I pay my rent?

The rent is paid directly to the landlord, so you don’t have to pay anything to Student.com. The rent can typically be paid with either a bank transfer or a credit or debit card.

### Are the properties furnished?

This depends on the property, but most of the places we list in Liverpool are rented fully furnished. You can check the property page to see if the property you’re interested in is rented fully furnished or not.

Property details

## Live close to your classes at St Andrews Gardens, within reach of Liverpool’s eclectic art spaces and the scenic Albert Dock

Read More

-   Address:
    
    21 Moor Place, Liverpool, L3 5XA
    
    View map
-   Distance to Liverpool John Moores University:
    
    -   5mins
    -   10mins
    -   4mins
    
-   Distance to University of Liverpool:
    
    -   11mins
    -   11mins
    -   4mins
    
-   Facilities: Kitchen, Furnished, Laundry, Refrigerator+10
    
-   Bills included: WiFi, Water, Electricity, Heating, Gas
    

At St Andrews Gardens, you’ll be living a short hop from the University of Liverpool. Before class, fuel up for the day with a top-notch full English breakfast in Lox & Caper café. Head over to the Walker Art Gallery after your lectures to see works by Rubens and Rembrandt, or check out the samurai armour and dinosaur casts at the World Museum. Then, wander down to Albert Dock to watch boats drifting along the river. Catch a show at the retro Epstein Theatre after dark, or dance all night to live music at Heebie Jeebies nightclub.

You’ll be based just two minutes from the city centre, so you’ll find it easy to get to Liverpool’s universities. Stroll seven minutes to reach the University of Liverpool and Liverpool John Moores University, or 10 to get to Liverpool Hope University. For classes at Liverpool Institute for Performing Arts, you can walk just 15 minutes from your door.

Back at St Andrews Gardens, you can head straight to the courtyard to get some fresh air and catch up on your reading. Then, join your neighbours in the common room to relax after a busy day, and sit down on a comfy chair to watch your favourite Sky shows on the TV.

Once you’ve worked up an appetite, head to your modern apartment. Cook with your housemates in the fitted kitchen. Sit down to eat at the breakfast bar, and kick back on the comfy sofa afterwards to relax. Some apartments come with flatscreen TVs, so you can spend your evening watching your favourite series.

When it’s time to hit the books, head to your private room to work on your assignments in peace. Spread your books out on your desk to get started, and connect to the free Wi-Fi to bounce your ideas off your classmates online.

With work out the way, get ready to meet your friends at Aloha Bar, where you can try their secret recipe cocktails. Freshen up with a shower in your bathroom, and choose an outfit from the wardrobe in your room. Rest easy knowing your belongings will be kept safe with CCTV and secure door entry, and there’s an on-site maintenance team to deal with any problems.

## Property Details

Description:

Get weekends off to a great start with breakfast at Bold Street Coffee, which is a 15-minute stroll from your student accommodation. Tuck into coconut porridge or avocado toast, or sip a flat white as you make plans with friends. Check out the boutiques in Metquarter, or head for the Waterfront to gaze at contemporary art at TATE Modern or photography at Open Eye Gallery. Later, eat pizza at nearby Dough Bar, and go dancing at Baa Bar.

It’s easy to get to class when you choose Apollo Court as your student housing in Liverpool. It’s a 10-minute walk to University of Liverpool and Liverpool John Moores University, and you can get to lectures in three minutes if you keep a bike in the secure storage and pedal to class.

After a long day on campus you’ll be happy to return to your student room. Enjoy your own space in a studio, or opt for an ensuite room with shared kitchen facilities. Whatever you choose, there’s a spacious common room where you can socialise with your new friends.

Use the onsite facilities to tackle your laundry, then head back to your room to connect to the free Wi-Fi and work on your latest assignment. Each room has a spacious study area where you can work in comfort, and there’s plenty of storage to keep your books and files in order. There’s onsite security and maintenance for your peace of mind.

We Will Help You Find Your Perfect Room!

## Property Details

Description:

Be part of a student community at the epicentre of Liverpool’s vibrant university district, just a short walk from Bold Street’s many cool bars and cafes. Stroll down and grab a morning latte while watching the world go by at hip hangout Bold Street Coffee, or admire the city skyline (including views of the historic St Luke’s Church) from the roof terrace at Hannah’s Bar. If their trademark cocktails aren’t your thing, spend an evening listening to live music in the beautiful surrounds of LEAF tearoom and bar before making the short walk home.

With Liverpool University, LJMU and LIPA all within just a 10-minute walk, Lennon Studios is part of a bustling student village. A short stroll from home and you’ll be in the lively city centre. If you’re feeling like venturing further afield on your days off, Lime Street station - linking to cities including Manchester and London - is only minutes away too.

But you won’t need to leave town at all, with so much to keep you busy. Take the short walk to the renowned Georgian Quarter and Bold Street, or hop on a bus to Albert Dock for a bite to eat with friends. You don’t even need to step outside your own front door for a good time. The heritage-listed residence’s own bar, The Font, is a firm favourite with locals, and for something more low-key, there’s a common room where you can hang out with friends. You’ll also find a convenience store onsite, perfect for when you’ve run out of essentials. For a bigger shop, take advantage of the parking and bike storage options available and make the short drive or ride to Tesco.

Wi-Fi, contents insurance and all utility bills are included, so you can budget instead for a splurge at the shops. The washer/dryer provided means you won’t even need to worry about paying for (or hauling laundry around to) a launderette.

When you’re not out exploring the city, you can always feel at ease knowing that while you’re at home, CCTV and secure door entry will help ensure your safety.

  

**\*1st-year students at Liverpool John Moore University will need to apply through the University for this property.**

## About Innovo House – Liverpool

Read More

-   Address:
    
    60 Devon St, Liverpool, L3 8AJ
    
    View map
-   Distance to Liverpool John Moores University:
    
    -   12mins
    -   3mins
    
-   Distance to Liverpool John Moores University(City Campus):
    
    -   15mins
    -   5mins
    
-   Facilities: Furnished, Laundry+8
    
-   Bills included: WiFi, Water, Electricity, Heating, Gas+2
    

Welcome to our brand new student accommodation in Liverpool: Innovo. Located in the heart of the city, Innovo is ideal for all students due to its location close to the universities.

-   Liverpool John Moores University: 5-minute walk
-   University of Liverpool – all campuses: 1 mile away
-   [L](https://web.archive.org/web/20241012124827/https://www.hope.ac.uk/lifeathope/ourcampuses/creativecampus/)iverpool Hope University Creative campus: 1 mile away

With a selection of modern en-suite rooms and studios, Innovo has a room to suit your taste and budget. Each room boasts a private en-suite, study area, and a double bed, providing the perfect environment to relax and study. Each studio comes with its own TV and TV license, and en-suite shared kitchens also come with their own TV.

Innovo has a number of areas for you to unwind in your spare time. You can go head-to-head with your friends in the games room or simply unwind with your mates in the communal lounge. Innovo also has on-site management and 24/7 security to ensure that you feel safe and secure.

If you’re looking for modern student accommodation in the heart of Liverpool, then Innovo is the place for you. You’ll be surrounded by plenty of bars, restaurants, shops, as well as the universities. Make no mistake, book now, and secure your room at Innovo today!

–

## Booking process

Submit an application

Speak with your consultant

Booking confirmation

**Submit an application:** Let us know your request needs and contact information. Don't worry if you're unsure of your dates/school yet, just let us know

**Speak with your consultant:** You'll be paired with a specialized booking consultant, ask away! Let him/her know more about what you're looking for

**Booking confirmation:** Complete the booking application form and other property-specific documents, and then we'll help you confirm your booking

## Liverpool

## Student accommodation in Liverpool

With a large student population and culture and nightlife scenes that deliver attractive options in spades, Liverpool is one of the most loved student cities in the UK. The city is considered one of the most affordable in the region and Student.com can help you easily find the right student accommodation for your budget.

You can utilise our search filters to find your favourite from more than 50 different student accommodation options in Liverpool. You can also use our mapping tool to find apartments in the area of the city you like, whether you want to live in the city centre or right next to your university.

If you need any more information, you can always give us a call or talk to us via the live chat function. Our booking consultants are always happy to help you and answer any questions you may have.

## A level results day 2022 in Liverpool

A level results day is on 18 August 2022. This is the day when British students finishing high school receive their finals results and find out which university they have been accepted to. This means that a very large number of first year students will be booking their student accommodation on, and immediately after, this date.

Liverpool is one of the most popular cities in the UK to study in, so many properties we list may sell out fast during this period. If you’re looking to study in Liverpool during the 2022/23 academic year, make sure to book early to have the best availability. Our booking consultants have the most up-to-date information about what’s available, so get in touch and we’ll help you find the perfect student home for you!

Many of the properties we list in Liverpool have a **No Place No Pay** offer in place. This means that you can book before results day with total peace of mind, because if you don’t get the offer you were expecting, you can cancel your accommodation and get your money back.

## UCAS clearing 2022 in Liverpool

If you didn’t get the grades you were hoping for and haven’t received any offers from universities, you can still find a place to study through UCAS Clearing. Clearing is a process that lets universities list courses where they have extra places available.

Clearing for 2022 has already started, so if you didn’t receive any offers, you can use it to find courses where there are places available. This way you can still go to university this autumn, even if you didn’t get any offers based on your A level results. In Liverpool at least these universities have offered places through Clearing in 2022:

-   [University of Liverpool](https://web.archive.org/web/20220819235353/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/university-of-liverpool)
-   [Liverpool John Moores University](https://web.archive.org/web/20220819235353/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/liverpool-john-moores-university-main-campus)
-   [Liverpool Hope University](https://web.archive.org/web/20220819235353/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/liverpool-hope-university)

## Liverpool at a glance

Liverpool, hometown of the legendary Beatles, is a city and metropolitan borough in Merseyside, England. In addition to one of the most influential bands of all time, this iconic city has a lot of other things to offer as well.

With a grand backdrop of Victorian and Georgian buildings, it’s an intimate and vibrant city that celebrates its glorious past. It’s home to many famous landmarks such as the homes of The Beatles members, The Liver Buildings, and the historic docks – all of which will become familiar sights if you choose to study in the city.

The city also values friendship. Liverpool is one of the friendliest cities in the UK and the third best to visit worldwide according to the Rough Guides guidebooks. Whether the local people are helping you find your way around the city, or just having a chat, the Scousers, as they’re affectionately called, will make your time in the city a memorable one.

### Football in Liverpool

A huge part of Liverpool’s worldwide fame is thanks to its football. Liverpool is proud of its undying love for the sport. It’s home to one of football's most famous rivalries, the Merseyside Derby between Liverpool and Everton, two storied clubs in the English Premier League. Liverpool FC is one of the most successful teams in England and Europe.

Even if you’re not a hardcore football fan, don’t miss out on the chance to see a Premier League game at one of the city’s famous stadiums, Liverpool FC’s Anfield or Everton’s Goodison Park. You can be sure that the atmosphere will be great.

### A city of culture

Liverpool is a cultural hotspot. Outside of London, it has more museums and art galleries than any city in the UK. From the Tate Modern and its world-famous collection of modern art to the live music and performances of The East Village Arts Club and the RIBA award-winning theatre The Everyman, just to name a few, it has cultural interests to meet all needs.

Liverpool wears its culture proudly. This a city that turned it’s bombed-out church into a concert venue, and has a night specifically dedicated to wandering around and looking at various light installations throughout the city.

The city also has the oldest Chinese community in Europe. The cultural vibrancy of Liverpool augments its environment, allowing new students to easily connect and interact with the city.

## Student life in Liverpool

There are several things that make Liverpool a great city to study in. It’s laid-back, fun and affordable, and if you want to have a great party after a long week of studying, Liverpool is definitely the place for you.

### Liverpool is an affordable city

One of the most important aspects of choosing a city to study in is its affordability. Liverpool is one of the most affordable cities in the UK. There are student discounts offered in most bars and clubs and if you happen to have to take a cab or bus to get there it won’t cost you much as taxis and buses are very affordable. Buses also run frequently so you won’t be stuck waiting for ages.

### Free museums and student discounts

Many of Liverpool’s museums and art galleries can be entered for free by students including Tate Liverpool, Walker Art Gallery, Merseyside Maritime Museum, World Museum and the Museum of Liverpool. The Albert Docks, home to award-winning attractions like The Beatles Story and The International Slavery Museum, always has free events.

Many of the big-name shops in Liverpool’s compact central shopping district provide student discounts ranging from 10% to 20%.

### Great nightlife

Liverpool is known for its laid-back way of life but it comes alive at night. Its vibrant nightlife offers many choices for all tastes. There are bars galore from Concert Square all the way to the Cavern Quarter. If you're looking for a good student night out there’s somewhere to go for each day of the week.

There are many music venues where you can listen to some live music ranging from the most in-demand musicians to up-and-coming artists. If you prefer a less-than-typical night out experience, the warehouse scene in the Baltic Triangle provides several options. Alma de Cuba, a bar in a former church, as well as the multitude of secret bars like Berry and Rye and Ex-Directory also provide less-than-typical experiences.

A large part of Liverpool’s nightlife is centred around three main areas - the centre of town, Lark Lane and the Baltic Triangle, where you’ll find some of the best cocktails, live music, and general revelry.

However, Smithdown Road, whose junction with Penny Lane is the subject of the Beatles song "Penny Lane," is home to a large percentage of Liverpool's 60,000-plus university student population and is always brimming with energy. Here you can have fun with fellow students as well as some delightful local Scousers at the Evil Eye Burrito Shack and cheap pints at Brookhouse on Thursdays at the long-established student quarter.

Overall, Liverpool’s nightlife is student-friendly. Venues are easy to get to as the majority of the student bars are within walking distance of each other.

## Universities in Liverpool

Liverpool is home to two world-class universities, with both the University of Liverpool and Liverpool John Moores University featured in the QS World University Rankings.

The University of Liverpool has almost 30,000 students, of whom almost 10,000 are from abroad. It was ranked as the 190th best university in the world in the 2023 QS World University Rankings.

Liverpool John Moores University has about 25,000 students, over 3,000 of whom are from outside the UK. So, if you’re looking for an international atmosphere while studying, you’ll be sure to find it here. John Moores was also ranked as one of the 1,000 best universities in the world by QS in their 2023 rankings.

In addition to these two, there are also numerous colleges and the famous Liverpool Institute for Performing Arts. Some of the most famous institutions of higher learning in Liverpool include:

-   [University of Liverpool](https://web.archive.org/web/20220819235353/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/university-of-liverpool)
-   [Liverpool John Moores University](https://web.archive.org/web/20220819235353/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/liverpool-john-moores-university-main-campus)
-   [Liverpool Hope University](https://web.archive.org/web/20220819235353/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/liverpool-hope-university)
-   [Liverpool Institute for Performing Arts](https://web.archive.org/web/20220819235353/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/liverpool-institute-for-performing-arts)
-   [Liverpool International College](https://web.archive.org/web/20220819235353/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/liverpool-international-college)

## Frequently asked questions about student housing in Liverpool

### How do I apply for student accommodation on Student.com?

Booking a student residence in Liverpool is free and easy on Student.com. After you’ve found your ideal uni accommodation in Liverpool, click ‘View rooms’ to go to the property page. There you’ll need to choose your preferred room type and click ‘Enquire’ or ‘Book Now.’

One of our booking consultants will then contact you to take you through the next steps and answer any questions you may have.

### What are the different room types you offer?

We currently offer two different types of rooms that you can choose from in Liverpool.

In a Private Room, you’ll get your own private bedroom and, in some properties, a private bathroom as well. However, in some properties, the bathroom is shared. Additional facilities like the kitchen will be shared.

Booking the Entire Place will give you a fully self-contained studio property with your own bedroom, bathroom and usually a small kitchenette for cooking meals. No need to share with anyone, so this option is perfect if you love your own space!

### Can I live together with a friend?

Yes. Tell your booking consultant that you’d like to live with a friend, and we can arrange this. Make sure your friend does the same when making their booking as well.

### Can I see the property before I move in?

Many of the properties we list have a great range of photos, videos and even virtual tours that will give you a great idea of what your new home will look like. So, even if you can’t make it to a viewing before moving in, you don’t have to worry, as you’ll be able to get a good idea of what your new home will look like.

If you’ll be in Liverpool before your move-in date and would prefer to see the place for yourself though, this can be arranged as well. Just get in touch with us and our booking consultants will set up a viewing for you.

### How do I pay my rent?

The rent is paid directly to the landlord, so you don’t have to pay anything to Student.com. The rent can typically be paid with either a bank transfer or a credit or debit card.

### Are the properties furnished?

This depends on the property, but most of the places we list in Liverpool are rented fully furnished. You can check the property page to see if the property you’re interested in is rented fully furnished or not.

## Liverpool

## Student accommodation in Liverpool

With a large student population and culture and nightlife scenes that deliver attractive options in spades, Liverpool is one of the most loved student cities in the UK. The city is considered one of the most affordable in the region and Student.com can help you easily find the right student accommodation for your budget.

You can utilise our search filters to find your favourite from more than 50 different student accommodation options in Liverpool. You can also use our mapping tool to find apartments in the area of the city you like, whether you want to live in the city centre or right next to your university.

If you need any more information, you can always give us a call or talk to us via the live chat function. Our booking consultants are always happy to help you and answer any questions you may have.

## A level results day 2022 in Liverpool

A level results day is on 18 August 2022. This is the day when British students finishing high school receive their finals results and find out which university they have been accepted to. This means that a very large number of first year students will be booking their student accommodation on, and immediately after, this date.

Liverpool is one of the most popular cities in the UK to study in, so many properties we list may sell out fast during this period. If you’re looking to study in Liverpool during the 2022/23 academic year, make sure to book early to have the best availability. Our booking consultants have the most up-to-date information about what’s available, so get in touch and we’ll help you find the perfect student home for you!

Many of the properties we list in Liverpool have a **No Place No Pay** offer in place. This means that you can book before results day with total peace of mind, because if you don’t get the offer you were expecting, you can cancel your accommodation and get your money back.

## UCAS clearing 2022 in Liverpool

If you didn’t get the grades you were hoping for and haven’t received any offers from universities, you can still find a place to study through UCAS Clearing. Clearing is a process that lets universities list courses where they have extra places available.

Clearing for 2022 has already started, so if you didn’t receive any offers, you can use it to find courses where there are places available. This way you can still go to university this autumn, even if you didn’t get any offers based on your A level results. In Liverpool at least these universities have offered places through Clearing in 2022:

-   [University of Liverpool](https://web.archive.org/web/20220815185013/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/university-of-liverpool)
-   [Liverpool John Moores University](https://web.archive.org/web/20220815185013/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/liverpool-john-moores-university-main-campus)
-   [Liverpool Hope University](https://web.archive.org/web/20220815185013/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/liverpool-hope-university)

## Liverpool at a glance

Liverpool, hometown of the legendary Beatles, is a city and metropolitan borough in Merseyside, England. In addition to one of the most influential bands of all time, this iconic city has a lot of other things to offer as well.

With a grand backdrop of Victorian and Georgian buildings, it’s an intimate and vibrant city that celebrates its glorious past. It’s home to many famous landmarks such as the homes of The Beatles members, The Liver Buildings, and the historic docks – all of which will become familiar sights if you choose to study in the city.

The city also values friendship. Liverpool is one of the friendliest cities in the UK and the third best to visit worldwide according to the Rough Guides guidebooks. Whether the local people are helping you find your way around the city, or just having a chat, the Scousers, as they’re affectionately called, will make your time in the city a memorable one.

### Football in Liverpool

A huge part of Liverpool’s worldwide fame is thanks to its football. Liverpool is proud of its undying love for the sport. It’s home to one of football's most famous rivalries, the Merseyside Derby between Liverpool and Everton, two storied clubs in the English Premier League. Liverpool FC is one of the most successful teams in England and Europe.

Even if you’re not a hardcore football fan, don’t miss out on the chance to see a Premier League game at one of the city’s famous stadiums, Liverpool FC’s Anfield or Everton’s Goodison Park. You can be sure that the atmosphere will be great.

### A city of culture

Liverpool is a cultural hotspot. Outside of London, it has more museums and art galleries than any city in the UK. From the Tate Modern and its world-famous collection of modern art to the live music and performances of The East Village Arts Club and the RIBA award-winning theatre The Everyman, just to name a few, it has cultural interests to meet all needs.

Liverpool wears its culture proudly. This a city that turned it’s bombed-out church into a concert venue, and has a night specifically dedicated to wandering around and looking at various light installations throughout the city.

The city also has the oldest Chinese community in Europe. The cultural vibrancy of Liverpool augments its environment, allowing new students to easily connect and interact with the city.

## Student life in Liverpool

There are several things that make Liverpool a great city to study in. It’s laid-back, fun and affordable, and if you want to have a great party after a long week of studying, Liverpool is definitely the place for you.

### Liverpool is an affordable city

One of the most important aspects of choosing a city to study in is its affordability. Liverpool is one of the most affordable cities in the UK. There are student discounts offered in most bars and clubs and if you happen to have to take a cab or bus to get there it won’t cost you much as taxis and buses are very affordable. Buses also run frequently so you won’t be stuck waiting for ages.

### Free museums and student discounts

Many of Liverpool’s museums and art galleries can be entered for free by students including Tate Liverpool, Walker Art Gallery, Merseyside Maritime Museum, World Museum and the Museum of Liverpool. The Albert Docks, home to award-winning attractions like The Beatles Story and The International Slavery Museum, always has free events.

Many of the big-name shops in Liverpool’s compact central shopping district provide student discounts ranging from 10% to 20%.

### Great nightlife

Liverpool is known for its laid-back way of life but it comes alive at night. Its vibrant nightlife offers many choices for all tastes. There are bars galore from Concert Square all the way to the Cavern Quarter. If you're looking for a good student night out there’s somewhere to go for each day of the week.

There are many music venues where you can listen to some live music ranging from the most in-demand musicians to up-and-coming artists. If you prefer a less-than-typical night out experience, the warehouse scene in the Baltic Triangle provides several options. Alma de Cuba, a bar in a former church, as well as the multitude of secret bars like Berry and Rye and Ex-Directory also provide less-than-typical experiences.

A large part of Liverpool’s nightlife is centred around three main areas - the centre of town, Lark Lane and the Baltic Triangle, where you’ll find some of the best cocktails, live music, and general revelry.

However, Smithdown Road, whose junction with Penny Lane is the subject of the Beatles song "Penny Lane," is home to a large percentage of Liverpool's 60,000-plus university student population and is always brimming with energy. Here you can have fun with fellow students as well as some delightful local Scousers at the Evil Eye Burrito Shack and cheap pints at Brookhouse on Thursdays at the long-established student quarter.

Overall, Liverpool’s nightlife is student-friendly. Venues are easy to get to as the majority of the student bars are within walking distance of each other.

## Universities in Liverpool

Liverpool is home to two world-class universities, with both the University of Liverpool and Liverpool John Moores University featured in the QS World University Rankings.

The University of Liverpool has almost 30,000 students, of whom almost 10,000 are from abroad. It was ranked as the 190th best university in the world in the 2023 QS World University Rankings.

Liverpool John Moores University has about 25,000 students, over 3,000 of whom are from outside the UK. So, if you’re looking for an international atmosphere while studying, you’ll be sure to find it here. John Moores was also ranked as one of the 1,000 best universities in the world by QS in their 2023 rankings.

In addition to these two, there are also numerous colleges and the famous Liverpool Institute for Performing Arts. Some of the most famous institutions of higher learning in Liverpool include:

-   [University of Liverpool](https://web.archive.org/web/20220815185013/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/university-of-liverpool)
-   [Liverpool John Moores University](https://web.archive.org/web/20220815185013/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/liverpool-john-moores-university-main-campus)
-   [Liverpool Hope University](https://web.archive.org/web/20220815185013/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/liverpool-hope-university)
-   [Liverpool Institute for Performing Arts](https://web.archive.org/web/20220815185013/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/liverpool-institute-for-performing-arts)
-   [Liverpool International College](https://web.archive.org/web/20220815185013/https://www.student.com/uk/liverpool/u/liverpool-international-college)

## Frequently asked questions about student housing in Liverpool

### How do I apply for student accommodation on Student.com?

Booking a student residence in Liverpool is free and easy on Student.com. After you’ve found your ideal uni accommodation in Liverpool, click ‘View rooms’ to go to the property page. There you’ll need to choose your preferred room type and click ‘Enquire’ or ‘Book Now.’

One of our booking consultants will then contact you to take you through the next steps and answer any questions you may have.

### What are the different room types you offer?

We currently offer two different types of rooms that you can choose from in Liverpool.

In a Private Room, you’ll get your own private bedroom and, in some properties, a private bathroom as well. However, in some properties, the bathroom is shared. Additional facilities like the kitchen will be shared.

Booking the Entire Place will give you a fully self-contained studio property with your own bedroom, bathroom and usually a small kitchenette for cooking meals. No need to share with anyone, so this option is perfect if you love your own space!

### Can I live together with a friend?

Yes. Tell your booking consultant that you’d like to live with a friend, and we can arrange this. Make sure your friend does the same when making their booking as well.

### Can I see the property before I move in?

Many of the properties we list have a great range of photos, videos and even virtual tours that will give you a great idea of what your new home will look like. So, even if you can’t make it to a viewing before moving in, you don’t have to worry, as you’ll be able to get a good idea of what your new home will look like.

If you’ll be in Liverpool before your move-in date and would prefer to see the place for yourself though, this can be arranged as well. Just get in touch with us and our booking consultants will set up a viewing for you.

### How do I pay my rent?

The rent is paid directly to the landlord, so you don’t have to pay anything to Student.com. The rent can typically be paid with either a bank transfer or a credit or debit card.

### Are the properties furnished?

This depends on the property, but most of the places we list in Liverpool are rented fully furnished. You can check the property page to see if the property you’re interested in is rented fully furnished or not.
